"Erynnis funeralis","2017-03-25 00:00:00 -0600","Funereal Duskywing (Erynnis funeralis)

25 March 2017
Tomás Rivera Elementary School
Denton, Denton County, Texas

This was a surprisingly excellent park area for documenting different kinds of moth and butterfly species at this time of the year. This Funereal Duskywing was feeding on the blossoms of Redstem Filaree (Erodium cicutarium).

"Erynnis funeralis","2015-07-16 00:00:00 -0800","Funereal Duskywing (Erynnis funeralis) , Skipper Butterfly

Never before recorded for Sonoma County in the Lepidopterists’ Society, it's soon to be added to their Season Summary for 2015 as a County Record.

It's a Duskywing skipper butterfly, which flew into our garden, like a dive bomber, landed on the purple Wallflower, long enough for me to take a few photos, then zoomed out as fast as he could.
 
Funereal Duskywing (Erynnis funeralis) is a butterfly of the Hesperididae family. It is found from Southern California, Arizona, New Mexico & Texas south to Argentina & Chile.
